Kelly's career has stretched from making perfect party bangers to bewildering operas. From the first chapter of his undeniable masterpiece Trapped in the Closet, you know that you will never be the same again. It's easy to take shots at R. Kelly's hip-hopera, but only from a place of cowardice upon realizing you will never create anything of this magnitude. He rhymes \"dresser\" with \"Beretta.\" He throws in lines such as, \"I knew you would do some bogus shit up in my house,\" as sincere, heartfelt dialogue. He frequently notes that he is in \"some deep shit,\" with his trademark descending vocal slide.
